    # _nn_train_target_ptr, _nn_train_output_activations_ptr,
    # _nn_train_output_pre_activations_ptr, _nn_train_output_deltas_ptr

    # Loop through each neuron in the output layer
    0 AS _nn_delta_idx
    WHILE _nn_delta_idx _nn_train_target_ptr ARRAY.len < DO
        # 1. Calculate error = target - actual
        _nn_train_target_ptr _nn_delta_idx ARRAY.get
        _nn_train_output_activations_ptr _nn_delta_idx ARRAY.get
        FP.sub AS _nn_delta_error

        # 2. Calculate derivative = relu_derivative(pre_activation)
        _nn_train_output_pre_activations_ptr _nn_delta_idx ARRAY.get
        _NN.relu_derivative AS _nn_delta_derivative

        # 3. Calculate delta = error * derivative
        _nn_delta_error _nn_delta_derivative FP.mul

        # 4. Append the final delta to the output deltas array. This array
        #    will be used to calculate the hidden layer deltas next.
        _nn_train_output_deltas_ptr ARRAY.append

        _nn_delta_idx 1 + AS _nn_delta_idx
    DONE
}

# ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
# PRIVATE HELPER: _NN.calculate_hidden_deltas
# Calculates the error gradients (deltas) for the hidden layer.
# This is the second step of the backward pass.
#
# Formula: delta_h = (SUM(delta_o * weight_ho)) * relu_derivative(pre_act_h)
#
# Stack: ( hidden_layer_ptr, output_layer_ptr -- )
# ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
DEF _NN.calculate_hidden_deltas {
    # This function receives the layer pointers as arguments
    AS _nn_output_layer_ptr
    AS _nn_hidden_layer_ptr

    # Loop through each neuron in the hidden layer (h_idx)
    0 AS _nn_hidden_delta_idx
    WHILE _nn_hidden_delta_idx _nn_hidden_layer_ptr ARRAY.len < DO

        # Initialize the sum of weighted output deltas for this hidden neuron
        0 FP.from_int AS _nn_weighted_delta_sum

        # Loop through each neuron in the output layer (o_idx) to calculate the sum
        0 AS _nn_output_delta_idx
        WHILE _nn_output_delta_idx _nn_output_layer_ptr ARRAY.len < DO

            # Get the current output neuron
            _nn_output_layer_ptr _nn_output_delta_idx ARRAY.get AS _nn_perceptron_ptr

            # Get the weights array of the current output neuron
            _nn_perceptron_ptr 1 ARRAY.get AS _nn_weights_ptr

            # Get the specific weight connecting hidden_neuron[h_idx] to output_neuron[o_idx].
            # The index of this weight is h_idx.
            _nn_weights_ptr _nn_hidden_delta_idx ARRAY.get

            # Get the delta of the current output neuron
            _nn_train_output_deltas_ptr _nn_output_delta_idx ARRAY.get

            # Multiply them: delta_o * weight_ho
            FP.mul

            # Add to the running sum
            _nn_weighted_delta_sum FP.add AS _nn_weighted_delta_sum

            _nn_output_delta_idx 1 + AS _nn_output_delta_idx
        DONE

        # Get derivative for the current hidden neuron: relu_derivative(pre_activation_h)
        _nn_train_hidden_pre_activations_ptr _nn_hidden_delta_idx ARRAY.get _NN.relu_derivative

        # Final delta_h = weighted_delta_sum * derivative
        _nn_weighted_delta_sum FP.mul _nn_train_hidden_deltas_ptr ARRAY.append

        _nn_hidden_delta_idx 1 + AS _nn_hidden_delta_idx
    DONE
}

# ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
# PRIVATE HELPER: _NN.update_layer_weights
# Updates all weights and biases for a single layer using the calculated
# deltas. This is the final step of backpropagation.
#
# Stack: ( layer_ptr, deltas_ptr, inputs_ptr -- )
# ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
DEF _NN.update_layer_weights {
    # ( layer_ptr, deltas_ptr, inputs_ptr -- )
    AS _nn_update_inputs_ptr
    AS _nn_update_deltas_ptr
    AS _nn_update_layer_ptr

    # Loop through each neuron in the layer
    0 AS _nn_update_neuron_idx
    WHILE _nn_update_neuron_idx _nn_update_layer_ptr ARRAY.len < DO
        # Get the current neuron and its corresponding delta
        _nn_update_layer_ptr _nn_update_neuron_idx ARRAY.get AS _nn_perceptron_ptr
        _nn_update_deltas_ptr _nn_update_neuron_idx ARRAY.get AS _nn_update_delta

        # --- 1. Update Weights ---
        _nn_perceptron_ptr 1 ARRAY.get AS _nn_weights_ptr # Get weights array

        # Loop through each weight in the neuron
        0 AS _nn_update_weight_idx
        WHILE _nn_update_weight_idx _nn_weights_ptr ARRAY.len < DO
            # Get the input that corresponds to this weight
            _nn_update_inputs_ptr _nn_update_weight_idx ARRAY.get AS _nn_update_input

            # Calculate weight change: learning_rate * delta * input
            _nn_train_learning_rate _nn_update_delta FP.mul
            _nn_update_input FP.mul AS _nn_update_weight_change

            # Get current weight and calculate new weight
            _nn_weights_ptr _nn_update_weight_idx ARRAY.get
            _nn_update_weight_change FP.add AS _nn_update_new_value

            # Store the new weight back into the array
            _nn_update_new_value _nn_update_weight_idx _nn_weights_ptr ARRAY.put

            _nn_update_weight_idx 1 + AS _nn_update_weight_idx
        DONE

        # --- 2. Update Bias ---
        # The "input" for the bias is always 1, so the rule is simpler.
        # Calculate bias change: learning_rate * delta
        _nn_train_learning_rate _nn_update_delta FP.mul AS _nn_update_weight_change

        # Get current bias and calculate new bias
        _nn_perceptron_ptr 0 ARRAY.get
        _nn_update_weight_change FP.add AS _nn_update_new_value

        # Store the new bias back into the perceptron array
        _nn_update_new_value 0 _nn_perceptron_ptr ARRAY.put

        _nn_update_neuron_idx 1 + AS _nn_update_neuron_idx
    DONE
}


# ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
# PUBLIC API: NN.train
# Executes one full step of the backpropagation algorithm.
#
# Stack: (network_ptr, input_array_ptr, target_array_ptr, learning_rate -- )
# ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
# STRING forward_mess "  Forward pass..."
# STRING backward_mess "  Backward pass..."
# STRING update_mess "  Updating weights..."

DEF NN.train {
    # ( network_ptr, input_ptr, target_ptr, learning_rate -- )
    AS _nn_train_learning_rate
    AS _nn_train_target_ptr
    AS _nn_train_input_ptr
    AS _nn_network_ptr

    # ========================================================================
    # 1. FORWARD PASS
    #
    # Perform a full forward pass, but unlike NN.predict, we must store all
    # intermediate values (pre-activations and activations) as they are
    # needed for the backward pass calculations.
    # ========================================================================

    # forward_mess PRTstring

    # Clear all temporary arrays to prepare for the new training step
    _nn_train_hidden_pre_activations_ptr ARRAY.clear
    _nn_train_hidden_activations_ptr ARRAY.clear
    _nn_train_output_pre_activations_ptr ARRAY.clear
    _nn_train_output_activations_ptr ARRAY.clear
    _nn_train_output_deltas_ptr ARRAY.clear
    _nn_train_hidden_deltas_ptr ARRAY.clear

    # --- 1a. Hidden Layer Forward Pass ---
    _nn_network_ptr 1 ARRAY.get AS _nn_hidden_layer_ptr
    _nn_hidden_layer_ptr _nn_train_input_ptr _nn_train_hidden_pre_activations_ptr _nn_train_hidden_activations_ptr _NN.train_forward_pass_layer

    # --- 1b. Output Layer Forward Pass ---
    # The hidden layer's activations are the input to the output layer
    _nn_network_ptr 2 ARRAY.get AS _nn_output_layer_ptr
    _nn_output_layer_ptr _nn_train_hidden_activations_ptr _nn_train_output_pre_activations_ptr _nn_train_output_activations_ptr _NN.train_forward_pass_layer


    # ========================================================================
    # 2. BACKWARD PASS
    #
    # Calculate the error gradients (deltas) for each layer, starting from
    # the output and working backwards.
    # ========================================================================

    # backward_mess PRTstring

    # --- 2a. Calculate Output Layer Deltas ---
    # The error gradient for the output layer is:
    # delta = (target - actual) * relu_derivative(pre_activation)

    _NN.calculate_output_deltas

    # --- 2b. Calculate Hidden Layer Deltas ---
    # The error gradient for the hidden layer is more complex, as it's based
    # on the weighted sum of the deltas from the output layer.
    # delta_h = (SUM(delta_o * weight_ho)) * relu_derivative(pre_activation_h)

    _nn_hidden_layer_ptr _nn_output_layer_ptr _NN.calculate_hidden_deltas

    # ========================================================================
    # 3. UPDATE WEIGHTS
    #
    # Use the calculated deltas to update all weights and biases in the
    # network according to the rule:
    # new_weight = old_weight + learning_rate * delta * input_to_neuron
    # ========================================================================

    # update_mess PRTstring

    # --- 3a. Update Output Layer ---
    # The inputs to the output layer are the activations from the hidden layer.
    _nn_output_layer_ptr _nn_train_output_deltas_ptr _nn_train_hidden_activations_ptr _NN.update_layer_weights

    # --- 3b. Update Hidden Layer ---
    # The inputs to the hidden layer are the original inputs to the network.
    _nn_hidden_layer_ptr _nn_train_hidden_deltas_ptr _nn_train_input_ptr _NN.update_layer_weights


}

FILE: src/libs/nn_lib.stacks
------------------------------------------------------------
# ============================================================================
# Neural Network Library (nn_lib)
#
# Provides basic building blocks for neural networks, starting with a
# single perceptron.
#
# Depends on:
#   - array_lib: For dynamic data structures on the heap.
#   - fixed_point_lib: For handling fractional numbers (weights, bias).
# ============================================================================

USE std_heap
USE fixed_point_lib

VALUE num_inputs 0
VALUE weights_ptr 0
VALUE perceptron_ptr 0
VALUE i 0
VALUE input_val 0
VALUE input_ptr 0
VALUE weight_val 0
VALUE product 0
VALUE weighted_sum 0
VALUE bias 0
VALUE _error 0
VALUE error_fp 0
VALUE learning_rate 0
VALUE old_bias 0
VALUE old_weight 0
VALUE adjustment 0
VALUE weight_delta 0
VALUE new_bias 0
VALUE new_weight 0

# ============================================================================
# Perceptron Data Structure
#
# A perceptron is represented by a pointer to an array with 2 elements:
#   - Index 0: The bias (fixed-point).
#   - Index 1: A pointer to its weights array.
#
# The weights array has N elements, where N is the number of inputs.
# For this project, N=2 (for x and y coordinates).
# ============================================================================


# ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
# DEF NN.new_perceptron
# Creates a new perceptron with a given number of inputs.
#
# @param num_inputs The number of weights to create.
# @returns perceptron_ptr A pointer to the newly created perceptron structure.
# ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
DEF NN.new_perceptron {
    AS num_inputs

    # 1. Create the weights array and initialize with small random values
    num_inputs NEW.array AS weights_ptr
    0 AS i
    WHILE i num_inputs < DO
        # 1. Convert both integers to fixed-point before dividing
        RND 200 % 100 - FP.from_int # Convert random integer to fp
        1000 FP.from_int            # Convert 1000 to fp
        FP.div                      # Now divide the two fp numbers
        # 2. Append to array (stack is already in correct order: value, ptr)
        weights_ptr
        ARRAY.append
        i 1 + AS i
    DONE

    # 2. Create the main perceptron array (capacity 2: bias, weights_ptr)
    2 NEW.array AS perceptron_ptr

    # 3. Initialize bias to 0 and append to perceptron array
    0 FP.from_int perceptron_ptr ARRAY.append

    # 4. Append the pointer to the weights array
    weights_ptr perceptron_ptr ARRAY.append

    perceptron_ptr # Return the pointer to the new perceptron
}


# ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
# DEF NN.predict
# Calculates the weighted sum of inputs and returns the activated output.
# output = step( (w1*i1 + w2*i2 + ... + wN*iN) + bias )
#
# @param input_ptr Pointer to an array of fixed-point input values.
# @param perceptron_ptr Pointer to the perceptron to use for prediction.
# @returns guess The output of the activation function (1 or 0).
# ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
DEF NN.predict {
    AS perceptron_ptr
    AS input_ptr

    # 1. Get bias and weights_ptr from the perceptron structure
    0 perceptron_ptr ARRAY.get AS bias
    1 perceptron_ptr ARRAY.get AS weights_ptr

    # 2. Calculate the dot product (weighted sum)
    # Start with the bias
    bias AS weighted_sum
    0 AS i
    input_ptr ARRAY.len AS num_inputs
    WHILE i num_inputs < DO
        i input_ptr   ARRAY.get AS input_val
        i weights_ptr ARRAY.get AS weight_val

        input_val weight_val FP.mul AS product
        weighted_sum product FP.add AS weighted_sum

        i 1 + AS i
    DONE

    # 3. Apply the Step activation function
    # If weighted_sum > 0, output 1, else output 0
    weighted_sum 0 > IF 1 ELSE 0 END
}


# ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
# DEF NN.train_step
# Adjusts the perceptron's weights and bias based on the error.
# new_weight = old_weight + learning_rate * error * input
# new_bias = old_bias + learning_rate * error
#
# @param learning_rate A fixed-point value for the learning step size.
# @param error The calculated error (true_label - guess).
# @param input_ptr Pointer to the array of input values.
# @param perceptron_ptr Pointer to the perceptron to be trained.
# ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
DEF NN.train_step {
    AS perceptron_ptr
    AS input_ptr
    AS _error
    AS learning_rate

    # 1. Get pointers and data from the perceptron structure
    0 perceptron_ptr ARRAY.get AS old_bias
    1 perceptron_ptr ARRAY.get AS weights_ptr

    # 2. Calculate the update for the bias and apply it
    # new_bias = old_bias + learning_rate * error
    # Convert integer error to fixed-point before multiplication
    _error FP.from_int AS error_fp # error_fp is now a fixed-point number
    
    # Calculate the core adjustment: learning_rate * error
    learning_rate error_fp FP.mul AS adjustment
    
    old_bias adjustment FP.add AS new_bias
    new_bias 0 perceptron_ptr ARRAY.put

    # 3. Loop through weights and update each one
    # new_weight = old_weight + learning_rate * error * input
    0 AS i
    input_ptr ARRAY.len AS num_inputs
    WHILE i num_inputs < DO
        # Get the corresponding input value
        i input_ptr ARRAY.get AS input_val

        # Calculate the weight delta: learning_rate * error * input
        adjustment input_val FP.mul AS weight_delta

        # Get the old weight
        i weights_ptr ARRAY.get AS old_weight

        # Calculate and store the new weight
        old_weight weight_delta FP.add AS new_weight
        new_weight i weights_ptr ARRAY.put

        i 1 + AS i
    DONE
}


FILE: src/libs/parser_tools.stacks
------------------------------------------------------------
USE std_stern_io 
USE disk_utils

# Standard Parser and Tokenizer Library
# --- Private variables for TOKENIZE ---
# These act as private, static variables for the TOKENIZE function,
# ensuring its internal state does not interfere with the main Data Stack.
VALUE _strtok_s 0 # Holds the pointer to the start of the string
VALUE _strtok_d 0 # Holds the delimiter character
VALUE _strtok_p 0 # Holds the current pointer during the loop
VALUE _strtok_c 0 # Holds the current character for comparison

# --- TOKENIZE ---
# Splits a string by a delimiter. Modifies the string in-place.
# This is a simple and self-contained implementation.
#
# Usage:
#   &string delimiter TOKENIZE
#
# Stack before: &string, delimiter_char
# Stack after:  &token, &rest_of_string
#
# If delimiter is not found, &rest_of_string will be 0.
DEF TOKENIZE {
    # Pop inputs from the Data Stack and store them in our private variables
    AS _strtok_d
    AS _strtok_s

    # Advance _strtok_s past any leading delimiters
    :skip_delimiters_loop
        *_strtok_s AS _strtok_c
        _strtok_c 0 == IF
            # End of string, so no token
            0 # Push a null pointer for the token
            0 # Push a null pointer for the rest_of_string
            GOTO strtok_end
        END
        _strtok_c _strtok_d != IF
            # Found start of token
            GOTO find_end_of_token
        END
        _strtok_s 1 + AS _strtok_s
        GOTO skip_delimiters_loop

    :find_end_of_token
        # _strtok_s now points to the start of the token
        _strtok_s AS _strtok_p # Use _strtok_p to scan for the end

    :scan_loop
        *_strtok_p AS _strtok_c
        _strtok_c 0 == IF
            # End of string is end of token
            _strtok_s # Push the token pointer
            0         # Push a null pointer for the rest_of_string
            GOTO strtok_end
        END
        _strtok_c _strtok_d == IF
            # Found end of token
            0 AS *_strtok_p
            _strtok_s       # 1. The pointer to the token
            _strtok_p 1 +   # 2. The pointer to the rest of the string
            GOTO strtok_end
        END
        _strtok_p 1 + AS _strtok_p
        GOTO scan_loop

    :strtok_end
        # The two result pointers (&token, &rest_of_string) are now on the Data Stack.
}


# =============================================================================
# Bytecode Resources
# =============================================================================

# --- Bytecode Buffer ---
VAR bytecode_buffer 8704    # create buffer at adres 4096 - 512
VALUE bytecode_ptr 8704     # Pointer points to the start adres
VALUE current_opcode 1
VALUE current_value 1

# --- Opcodes ---
CONST OPC_END 0
CONST OPC_PUSH  1
CONST OPC_ADD   2
CONST OPC_PRINT 3
CONST OPC_UNKOWN 4
CONST OPC_USR 5
CONST OPC_STRING 6
CONST OPC_LOAD_FROM_DISK 7
CONST OPC_STACKINFO 8
# ... more opcodes will be added here


## Uses
# value opcode WRITE_TO_BYTECODE
# or
# opcode WRITE_TO_BYTECODE
#
# 

# --- WRITE_TO_BYTECODE ---
# Handles opcodes with and without arguments.
# Expects [opcode] on stack for simple opcodes.
# Expects [value, opcode] on stack for opcodes with arguments.
DEF WRITE_TO_BYTECODE {
    AS current_opcode # Pop opcode, leave value (if any)

    # Check if the opcode is one that takes an argument
    current_opcode OPC_PUSH == IF
        AS current_value # Pop the value from the stack
        current_opcode AS *bytecode_ptr
        bytecode_ptr 1 + AS bytecode_ptr
        current_value AS *bytecode_ptr
        bytecode_ptr 1 + AS bytecode_ptr
        GOTO write_to_bytecode_end
    END


    current_opcode OPC_UNKOWN == IF
        AS current_value # Pop the value from the stack
        current_opcode AS *bytecode_ptr
        bytecode_ptr 1 + AS bytecode_ptr
        current_value AS *bytecode_ptr
        bytecode_ptr 1 + AS bytecode_ptr
        GOTO write_to_bytecode_end
    END

    current_opcode OPC_STRING == IF
        AS current_value # Pop the value from the stack
        current_opcode AS *bytecode_ptr
        bytecode_ptr 1 + AS bytecode_ptr
        current_value AS *bytecode_ptr
        bytecode_ptr 1 + AS bytecode_ptr
        GOTO write_to_bytecode_end
    END

    # If not PUSH or UNKOWN/STRING, it's a simple opcode with no argument.
    # The stack should be empty now.
    current_opcode AS *bytecode_ptr
    bytecode_ptr 1 + AS bytecode_ptr
    
    :write_to_bytecode_end
}

# =============================================================================
# Bytecode Executor
# =============================================================================

##
# Start : &buffer_pointer EXECUTE_BYTECODE
# Program stops at OPC_END (null) termination
# No return values

VALUE bytecode_execution_ptr 3584
STRING ErrorMessage "Fatal error: an invalid token \n"
STRING InfoMessage0 "Total items on the stack: "
STRING InfoMessage1 "First value on the stack: "

DEF EXECUTE_BYTECODE {
    AS bytecode_execution_ptr

    :execution_loop
        # check for OPC_END, read the current opcode first
        *bytecode_execution_ptr AS current_opcode
        bytecode_execution_ptr 1 + AS bytecode_execution_ptr
        current_opcode OPC_END == IF
            GOTO execution_end
        END


        current_opcode OPC_PUSH == IF
            *bytecode_execution_ptr AS current_value
            bytecode_execution_ptr 1 + AS bytecode_execution_ptr
            current_value
            GOTO execution_loop
        END

        current_opcode OPC_STRING == IF
            *bytecode_execution_ptr AS current_value
            bytecode_execution_ptr 1 + AS bytecode_execution_ptr
            current_value
            GOTO execution_loop
        END

        current_opcode OPC_USR == IF
            ASM {
                ustack A $DATASTACK_PTR
                ld I A
                callx $_start_memory_
            }
            GOTO execution_loop
        END

        current_opcode OPC_LOAD_FROM_DISK == IF
            # "Load from disk routine " 
            # Expects an filename string pointer on the datastack

            DUP PRTstring 13 PRTchar
     
            load_bin_file

            GOTO execution_loop
        END


        current_opcode OPC_ADD == IF
            +
            GOTO execution_loop
        END

        current_opcode OPC_PRINT == IF
            PRINT
            # return PRTchar      # print an newline
            GOTO execution_loop
        END

        current_opcode OPC_STACKINFO == IF
            TOS.check IF
                TOS.check &InfoMessage0 PRTstring PRINT     ; Print stack depth
                DUP &InfoMessage1 PRTstring PRINT           ; Print first value (TOS)
            ELSE
                0 &InfoMessage0 PRTstring PRINT
            END
            GOTO execution_loop
        END


        current_opcode OPC_UNKOWN == IF
            # An OPC_UNKOWN has a value, so we need to skip it
            &ErrorMessage PRTstring
            bytecode_execution_ptr 1 + AS bytecode_execution_ptr
            GOTO execution_loop
        END

        &ErrorMessage PRTstring
        GOTO execution_end # Stop execution on error

    :execution_end
        
}





FILE: src/libs/rdp_lib.stacks
------------------------------------------------------------
# rdp_lib - Stern Light Reliable UDP Protocol
# Provides reliable messaging constants and structures.

USE socket_lib
USE std_heap
USE std_dict
USE std_time

# --- Message Types (Header[0]) ---
# Values > 128 to distinguish from ASCII SDP
CONST RDP_MSG_HELLO     129
CONST RDP_MSG_DATA      130
CONST RDP_MSG_ACK       131
CONST RDP_MSG_NACK      132
CONST RDP_MSG_STAT_REQ  133
CONST RDP_MSG_STAT_ACK  134
CONST RDP_MSG_STAT_QRY  135
CONST RDP_MSG_WAIT      136
CONST RDP_MSG_RESUME    137

# --- Connection States ---
# These states implicitly define what answer we expect.
CONST RDP_STATE_CLOSED    0   # Not active
CONST RDP_STATE_LISTEN    1   # Server: Waiting for HELLO
CONST RDP_STATE_INIT      2   # Client: Sent HELLO, Expecting STAT_ACK
CONST RDP_STATE_OPEN      3   # Connected: Normal DATA exchange
CONST RDP_STATE_WAIT      4   # Paused: Received WAIT, Expecting RESUME
CONST RDP_STATE_REQ       5   # Maintenance: Sent STAT_REQ, Expecting STAT_ACK

# --- Connection Record Layout ---
# A connection is a List of fixed size (16 words).
# We use offsets to access fields.
CONST RDP_CONN_SIZE       16

# Field Offsets
CONST RDP_PEER_ID     0   # Remote Host ID
CONST RDP_PEER_PORT   1   # Remote Port
CONST RDP_LOCAL_PORT  2   # Local Port binding
CONST RDP_STATE       3   # Current State (RDP_STATE_*)

# Sequence Numbers
CONST RDP_SEQ_OUT     4   # Next Seq Num to Send
CONST RDP_SEQ_IN      5   # Next Seq Num Expected (Recv)
CONST RDP_SEQ_ACK     6   # Last Seq Num ACKed by peer (What they have)

# Buffers
CONST RDP_TX_BUF      7   # Pointer to TX Dictionary (Sent but not ACKed)
CONST RDP_RX_BUF      8   # Pointer to RX Dictionary (Received out of order)

# Timing & Retries
CONST RDP_TIMER       9   # Timestamp of last action (for Timeout)
CONST RDP_RETRIES     10  # Retry counter
CONST RDP_RX_CONGESTED 11 # Flag: 1 if we sent WAIT, 0 if normal

# --- Library Globals ---
# Dictionary to hold active connection pointers, keyed by a composite of peer_id and peer_port.
# This is allocated on the heap during init.
VALUE _rdp_conns 0
# A reusable 2-word array for sending control packets to prevent heap allocation in loops.
VALUE _rdp_ctrl_packet 0
# A reusable buffer for receiving packets.
VALUE _rdp_recv_buf 0

# --- Internal Variables ---
# These are used as temporary storage within the library functions.
VALUE _conn 0
VALUE _conn_ptr 0
VALUE _new_conn 0
VALUE _key 0
VALUE _src_id 0
# VALUE _dest_id 0      ; Reused from socket_lib
# VALUE _dest_port 0    ; Reused from socket_lib
# VALUE _src_port 0     ; Reused from socket_lib
VALUE _local_port 0
VALUE _msg_type 0
VALUE _seq_num 0
VALUE _retries 0
VALUE _state 0
VALUE _current_state 0
VALUE _inbox 0
VALUE _can_send 0
# VALUE _count 0        ; Reused from std_heap
# VALUE _i 0            ; Reused from std_heap/socket_lib
VALUE _j 0
VALUE _payload_ptr 0
# VALUE _tmp_ptr 0      ; Reused from socket_lib

# A deque pool of reusable LISTs for storing packet data, to avoid heap fragmentation.
VALUE _rdp_packet_pool 0

VALUE _len 0
VALUE _data 0
VALUE _tx_buf 0
VALUE _tx_key 0
VALUE _pkt_seq 0
VALUE _pkt_buf 0
VALUE _last_sent 0
VALUE _resend_seq 0
VALUE _received_seq 0
STRING _rdp_err_pool "RDP.update: Packet Pool Exhausted!\n"

# Debug strings for RDP.print_status
STRING _str_rdp_status "--- RDP Status ---\n"
STRING _str_active_conn "Active Connections: "
STRING _str_conn "Conn "
STRING _str_colon ": "
STRING _str_state "State="
STRING _str_seq_out " SeqOUT="
STRING _str_seq_in " SeqIN="
STRING _str_tx_buf "   TxBuf Size="
STRING _str_rx_buf " RxBuf Size="
STRING _str_timer "   Timer="
STRING _str_retries " Retries="
STRING _str_rdp_footer "------------------\n"
STRING _str_newline "\n"


# Timeout settings
CONST RDP_TIMEOUT_MS 3500       # 3500 3.5 seconds timeout value
CONST RDP_MAX_RETRIES 10

# --- Packet Pool Configuration ---
CONST RDP_PACKET_POOL_SIZE 16  # Total number of reusable packet buffers TX windowsize + RX windowsize
CONST RDP_PACKET_SIZE      64  # Max size of an RDP packet list
CONST RDP_TX_WINDOW_SIZE    6 # Number of packets that can be in-flight before a STAT_REQ
CONST RDP_RX_WINDOW_SIZE   10  # Size of the receiver's buffer before a WAIT is sent

# ( -- )
DEF RDP.init {
    # 1. Allocate the connection dictionary on the heap.
    # Initial size of 8 is a suggestion for the hash table.
    8 DICT.new AS _rdp_conns            ; holds max 8 connection records
    
    # 2. Allocate reusable control and receive buffers.
    2 NEW.array AS _rdp_ctrl_packet     ; Used for sending Control packages
    256 NEW.array AS _rdp_recv_buf

    # 3. Create and populate the packet pool.
    DEQUE.new AS _rdp_packet_pool
    0 AS _i
    WHILE _i RDP_PACKET_POOL_SIZE < DO
        RDP_PACKET_SIZE NEW.array   # Create a new array of 64 words
        _rdp_packet_pool DEQUE.append # Add its pointer to the pool
        _i 1 + AS _i
    DONE

    
}

# Internal helper to create a lookup key from peer_id and peer_port.
# ( peer_id peer_port -- key )
DEF _rdp_make_key {
    # We multiply the peer_id by 65536 (shift left 16 bits) to avoid collisions
    # with the port number range (0-65535).
    # Stack: peer_id peer_port
    SWAP 65536 * +
}

# Internal helper: Calculate the previous sequence number (modulo logic)
# ( seq_num -- prev_seq_num )
DEF _rdp_prev_seq {
    # In our simple protocol with incrementing integers, previous is just -1.
    # If we had wrapping at 65535, we'd handle it here.
    1 -
}

# --- Internal Helpers ---

# _rdp_get_buffer ( -- buffer_ptr | 0 )
# Acquires a reusable packet buffer from the global pool.
# Returns 0 if the pool is exhausted.
DEF _rdp_get_buffer {
    _rdp_packet_pool DEQUE.is_empty IF
        0 # Pool is empty, return failure
    ELSE
        _rdp_packet_pool DEQUE.pop
    END
}

# _rdp_release_buffer ( buffer_ptr -- )
# Returns a packet buffer to the global pool.
# Does nothing if the provided pointer is 0.
DEF _rdp_release_buffer {
    DUP 0 != IF
        _rdp_packet_pool DEQUE.append
    ELSE
        DROP # Drop the 0 pointer
    END
}


# _rdp_send_raw_ctrl_packet ( conn_ptr msg_type seq_num -- success_flag )
# Low-level helper to send a control packet with a specific sequence number.
DEF _rdp_send_raw_ctrl_packet {
    AS _seq_num
    AS _msg_type
    AS _conn

    RDP_PEER_ID    _conn LIST.get AS _dest_id
    RDP_PEER_PORT  _conn LIST.get AS _dest_port
    RDP_LOCAL_PORT _conn LIST.get AS _src_port

    # Create the RDP packet [Type, SeqNum] as a temporary array
    _rdp_ctrl_packet ARRAY.clear
    _msg_type _rdp_ctrl_packet ARRAY.append
    _seq_num _rdp_ctrl_packet ARRAY.append

    # Send using the socket library's list sender
    _rdp_ctrl_packet _dest_id _dest_port _src_port SOCKET.snd_list
    ASM {
        nop
    }
}

# _rdp_send_control_packet ( conn_ptr msg_type -- success_flag )
# Sends a sender-initiated control packet (HELLO, STAT_REQ) using RDP_SEQ_OUT.
DEF _rdp_send_control_packet {
    AS _msg_type
    AS _conn
    RDP_SEQ_OUT _conn LIST.get AS _seq_num
    _conn _msg_type _seq_num _rdp_send_raw_ctrl_packet
}

# _rdp_send_response_packet ( conn_ptr msg_type -- success_flag )
# Sends a receiver-initiated packet (NACK, STAT_ACK) using the LAST received sequence number.
# Uses _rdp_prev_seq on RDP_SEQ_IN.
DEF _rdp_send_response_packet {
    AS _msg_type
    AS _conn
    RDP_SEQ_IN _conn LIST.get _rdp_prev_seq AS _seq_num
    _conn _msg_type _seq_num _rdp_send_raw_ctrl_packet
}

# _rdp_check_timeout ( conn_ptr -- )
# Checks if the connection has timed out and handles retransmission.
DEF _rdp_check_timeout {
    AS _conn

    # 1. Check delta time
    TIME.uptime 
    RDP_TIMER _conn LIST.get -
    RDP_TIMEOUT_MS > IF
        # --- Timeout Expired ---
        
        # 2. Check Max Retries
        RDP_RETRIES _conn LIST.get AS _retries
        _retries RDP_MAX_RETRIES > IF
            # Too many retries, close connection.
            RDP_STATE_CLOSED RDP_STATE _conn LIST.put
            # TODO: Notify application of error?
        ELSE
            # 3. Increment Retry Counter
            _retries 1 + RDP_RETRIES _conn LIST.put
            
            # 4. Reset Timer
            TIME.uptime RDP_TIMER _conn LIST.put

            # 5. Handle State-Specific Retransmission
            RDP_STATE _conn LIST.get AS _state
            
            _state RDP_STATE_INIT == IF
                # Resend HELLO
                _conn RDP_MSG_HELLO _rdp_send_control_packet DROP
            ELSE
                _state RDP_STATE_OPEN == IF
                    # Watchdog: Send STAT_QRY to check connection
                    _conn RDP_MSG_STAT_QRY _rdp_send_response_packet DROP
                ELSE
                    _state RDP_STATE_REQ == IF
                         # Resend STAT_REQ (Keep-alive or Poll)
                        _conn RDP_MSG_STAT_REQ _rdp_send_control_packet DROP
                    ELSE
                        _state RDP_STATE_WAIT == IF
                            # Probe: Send STAT_REQ to check if receiver is ready
                            _conn RDP_MSG_STAT_REQ _rdp_send_control_packet DROP
                        END
                    END
                END
            END
        END
    END
}

# --- Public API ---

# Internal Helper: Allocates and registers a connection record.
# ( dest_id dest_port local_port -- conn_ptr )
DEF _rdp_alloc_conn {
    AS _local_port
    AS _dest_port
    AS _dest_id

    # 1. Allocate Connection Record
    RDP_CONN_SIZE NEW.list AS _conn

    # 2. Set Header Fields
    _dest_id    RDP_PEER_ID    _conn LIST.put
    _dest_port  RDP_PEER_PORT  _conn LIST.put
    _local_port RDP_LOCAL_PORT _conn LIST.put
    
    # 3. Set State to INIT (Default, caller might change this)
    RDP_STATE_INIT RDP_STATE _conn LIST.put
    
    # 4. Initialize Counters (Zero out)
    1 RDP_SEQ_OUT _conn LIST.put
    1 RDP_SEQ_IN  _conn LIST.put
    0 RDP_SEQ_ACK _conn LIST.put
    TIME.uptime RDP_TIMER _conn LIST.put
    0 RDP_RETRIES _conn LIST.put
    0 RDP_RX_CONGESTED _conn LIST.put

    # 5. Initialize Buffers (Dictionaries of size 10)
    RDP_TX_WINDOW_SIZE DICT.new RDP_TX_BUF _conn LIST.put
    RDP_RX_WINDOW_SIZE DICT.new RDP_RX_BUF _conn LIST.put

    # 6. Register in Global Table
    _conn _dest_port _local_port _rdp_make_key _rdp_conns DICT.put
    
    _conn
}

# RDP.connect ( dest_id dest_port local_port -- conn_ptr 1 | 0 )
# Establishes a new reliable connection to a peer by creating a connection record.
# This is a public API function for client applications.
DEF RDP.connect {
    # 1. Allocate Record (Consumes args)
    _rdp_alloc_conn AS _conn
    
    # 2. Send HELLO packet to initiate handshake.
    _conn RDP_MSG_HELLO _rdp_send_control_packet
    
    IF
        _conn 1
    ELSE
        0
    END
}


VALUE _expected_seq 0
VALUE _rx_pkt 0

# RDP.update ( inbox_deque -- )
# This is the main engine of the RDP protocol. It should be called
# frequently in the application's main loop. It polls for incoming
# packets and updates the state machine for all connections.
DEF RDP.update {
    AS _inbox

    # 1. Poll for a new packet using the provided inbox.
    _rdp_recv_buf _inbox SOCKET.read IF
        # Packet received. Check if it's an RDP packet.
        _rdp_recv_buf MESSAGE.payload_ptr AS _payload_ptr
        *_payload_ptr AS _msg_type

        _msg_type 128 > IF
            # --- It's an RDP Packet ---
            _rdp_recv_buf MESSAGE.src       AS _src_id
            _rdp_recv_buf MESSAGE.src_port  AS _src_port
            _rdp_recv_buf MESSAGE.dest_port AS _local_port

            # 2. Find the connection record.
            _src_port _local_port _rdp_make_key AS _key

            _key _rdp_conns DICT.has_key IF
                # --- Scenario: Existing connection found ---
                _key _rdp_conns DICT.get AS _conn
                
                # Any packet from the peer is a sign of life. Reset Watchdog.
                TIME.uptime RDP_TIMER _conn LIST.put
                0 RDP_RETRIES _conn LIST.put

                _msg_type RDP_MSG_HELLO == IF
                    # --- Scenario: Remote Peer Restart / Re-connect ---
                    # Always accept HELLO on existing connections as a reset request.
                    _payload_ptr 1 + AS _tmp_ptr
                    *_tmp_ptr DUP
                    RDP_SEQ_IN _conn LIST.put
                    RDP_SEQ_OUT _conn LIST.put
                    RDP_STATE_OPEN RDP_STATE _conn LIST.put
                    _conn RDP_MSG_STAT_ACK _rdp_send_control_packet DROP
                ELSE
                    _msg_type RDP_MSG_WAIT == IF
                        # --- Handle WAIT ---
                        # Receiver buffer is full. Pause sending.
                        RDP_STATE_WAIT RDP_STATE _conn LIST.put
                        TIME.uptime RDP_TIMER _conn LIST.put
                    ELSE
                    _msg_type RDP_MSG_RESUME == IF
                        # --- Handle RESUME ---
                        # Receiver has space. Resume sending.

                        
                        # RDP_STATE_OPEN RDP_STATE _conn LIST.put
                        RDP_STATE_REQ RDP_STATE _conn LIST.put
                        
                        # 1. Cleanup Tx Buffer: Remove confirmed sequence range
                        _payload_ptr 1 + AS _tmp_ptr
                        *_tmp_ptr AS _received_seq

                        RDP_TX_BUF _conn LIST.get AS _tx_buf
                        RDP_SEQ_ACK _conn LIST.get 1 + AS _i
                        WHILE _i _received_seq 1 + < DO
                            _i _tx_buf DICT.has_key IF
                                _i _tx_buf DICT.get _rdp_release_buffer
                                _i _tx_buf DICT.remove
                            END
                            _i 1 + AS _i
                        DONE
                        _received_seq RDP_SEQ_ACK _conn LIST.put

                        # 2. Resend ALL remaining packets in Tx Buffer (Ordered by Sequence)
                        # Iterate from (LastAck + 1) to (NextToSend)
                        _seq_num 1 + AS _resend_seq
                        RDP_SEQ_OUT _conn LIST.get AS _len  # Reuse _len variable as limit
                        
                        WHILE _resend_seq _len < DO
                            _resend_seq _tx_buf DICT.has_key IF
                                _resend_seq _tx_buf DICT.get AS _pkt_buf
                                RDP_PEER_ID    _conn LIST.get AS _dest_id
                                RDP_PEER_PORT  _conn LIST.get AS _dest_port
                                RDP_LOCAL_PORT _conn LIST.get AS _src_port
                                _pkt_buf _dest_id _dest_port _src_port SOCKET.snd_list DROP
                            END
                            _resend_seq 1 + AS _resend_seq
                        DONE

                        # 3. Force Sync: Check if burst arrived safely
                        _conn RDP_MSG_STAT_REQ _rdp_send_control_packet DROP

                        # LET OP, not trusted yet!
                        TIME.uptime RDP_TIMER _conn LIST.put
                        0 RDP_RETRIES _conn LIST.put

                    ELSE
                    _msg_type RDP_MSG_STAT_ACK == IF
                        # --- Handle STAT_ACK ---
                        RDP_STATE _conn LIST.get AS _current_state
                        _current_state RDP_STATE_INIT == IF
                            # Our handshake is complete!
                            RDP_STATE_OPEN RDP_STATE _conn LIST.put
                            # Reset timer/retries here.
                            TIME.uptime RDP_TIMER _conn LIST.put
                            0 RDP_RETRIES _conn LIST.put
                        ELSE
                            # --- Sync / Tx Buffer Cleanup (Valid for OPEN and REQ) ---
                            _payload_ptr 1 + AS _tmp_ptr
                            *_tmp_ptr AS _received_seq # The Acked Seq Num

                            RDP_TX_BUF _conn LIST.get AS _tx_buf
                            
                            RDP_SEQ_ACK _conn LIST.get 1 + AS _i
                            WHILE _i _received_seq 1 + < DO
                                _i _tx_buf DICT.has_key IF
                                    _i _tx_buf DICT.get _rdp_release_buffer
                                    _i _tx_buf DICT.remove
                                END
                                _i 1 + AS _i
                            DONE
                            _received_seq RDP_SEQ_ACK _conn LIST.put

                            # If we were in REQ state (blocked), go back to OPEN
                            _current_state RDP_STATE_REQ == IF
                                RDP_STATE_OPEN RDP_STATE _conn LIST.put
                                TIME.uptime RDP_TIMER _conn LIST.put
                                0 RDP_RETRIES _conn LIST.put
                            END

                            # --- SYNC APPROACH: Fast Retransmit ---
                            # If peer is behind our last sent packet, push the next one.
                            RDP_SEQ_OUT _conn LIST.get 1 - AS _last_sent
                            _last_sent _received_seq > IF
                                # Peer needs seq_num + 1
                                _received_seq 1 + AS _key
                                
                                _key _tx_buf DICT.has_key IF
                                    _key _tx_buf DICT.get AS _pkt_buf
                                    RDP_PEER_ID    _conn LIST.get AS _dest_id
                                    RDP_PEER_PORT  _conn LIST.get AS _dest_port
                                    RDP_LOCAL_PORT _conn LIST.get AS _src_port
                                    _pkt_buf _dest_id _dest_port _src_port SOCKET.snd_list DROP
                                    _conn RDP_MSG_STAT_REQ _rdp_send_control_packet DROP
                                END
                            END
                        END
                    ELSE
                        _msg_type RDP_MSG_STAT_REQ == IF
                            # --- Handle STAT_REQ ---
                            # Sender requests status.
                            # If we are CONGESTED (Buffer Full), respond with WAIT instead of STAT_ACK
                            # to keep the sender paused.
                            RDP_RX_CONGESTED _conn LIST.get 1 == IF
                                _conn RDP_MSG_WAIT _rdp_send_response_packet DROP
                            ELSE
                                # Normal operation: Respond with STAT_ACK
                                _conn RDP_MSG_STAT_ACK _rdp_send_response_packet DROP
                            END
                        ELSE
                            _msg_type RDP_MSG_STAT_QRY == IF
                                # --- Handle STAT_QRY ---
                                # Peer asks "Are you there?". Check payload seq against our sent history.
                                _payload_ptr 1 + AS _tmp_ptr
                                *_tmp_ptr AS _seq_num

                                # # 1. Cleanup Buffer (They have up to _seq_num)
                                # RDP_TX_BUF _conn LIST.get AS _tx_buf
                                # 1 AS _i
                                # WHILE _i RDP_TX_WINDOW_SIZE 1 + < DO
                                #     _i _tx_buf DICT.has_key IF
                                #         _i _tx_buf DICT.get AS _pkt_buf
                                #         1 _pkt_buf ARRAY.get AS _pkt_seq
                                #         # Check if pkt_seq <= seq_num
                                #         _pkt_seq _seq_num > 0 == IF
                                #             _pkt_buf _rdp_release_buffer
                                #             _i _tx_buf DICT.remove
                                #         END
                                #     END
                                #     _i 1 + AS _i
                                # DONE

                                # 2. Check sync status
                                RDP_SEQ_OUT _conn LIST.get 1 - AS _last_sent 
                                _last_sent _seq_num == IF
                                    # In Sync: Send ACK
                                    _conn RDP_MSG_ACK _seq_num _rdp_send_raw_ctrl_packet DROP

                                    # Cleanup buffer this lookslike an better place for this
                                    RDP_TX_BUF _conn LIST.get AS _tx_buf
                                    RDP_SEQ_ACK _conn LIST.get 1 + AS _i
                                    WHILE _i _seq_num 1 + < DO
                                        _i _tx_buf DICT.has_key IF
                                            _i _tx_buf DICT.get _rdp_release_buffer
                                            _i _tx_buf DICT.remove
                                        END
                                        _i 1 + AS _i
                                    DONE
                                    _seq_num RDP_SEQ_ACK _conn LIST.put

                                    RDP_STATE_OPEN RDP_STATE _conn LIST.put # LET OP
                                ELSE
                                    # Out of Sync: Retransmit + STAT_REQ
                                    _seq_num 1 + AS _key
                                    
                                    _key _tx_buf DICT.has_key IF
                                        _key _tx_buf DICT.get AS _pkt_buf
                                        RDP_PEER_ID    _conn LIST.get AS _dest_id
                                        RDP_PEER_PORT  _conn LIST.get AS _dest_port
                                        RDP_LOCAL_PORT _conn LIST.get AS _src_port
                                        _pkt_buf _dest_id _dest_port _src_port SOCKET.snd_list DROP
                                        _conn RDP_MSG_STAT_REQ _rdp_send_control_packet DROP
                                    ELSE
                                        # Fallback if packet missing from buffer: just confirm what they have
                                        _conn RDP_MSG_ACK _seq_num _rdp_send_raw_ctrl_packet DROP
                                    END
                                    RDP_STATE_OPEN RDP_STATE _conn LIST.put
                                END
                            ELSE
                                _msg_type RDP_MSG_ACK == IF
                                    # --- Handle ACK ---
                                    # Ack received (from Watchdog or other). Clean up buffer.
                                    _payload_ptr 1 + AS _tmp_ptr
                                    *_tmp_ptr AS _seq_num

                                    RDP_TX_BUF _conn LIST.get AS _tx_buf
                                    RDP_SEQ_ACK _conn LIST.get 1 + AS _i
                                    WHILE _i _seq_num 1 + < DO
                                        _i _tx_buf DICT.has_key IF
                                            _i _tx_buf DICT.get _rdp_release_buffer
                                            _i _tx_buf DICT.remove
                                        END
                                        _i 1 + AS _i
                                    DONE
                                    _seq_num RDP_SEQ_ACK _conn LIST.put
                                    
                                    TIME.uptime RDP_TIMER _conn LIST.put
                                    0 RDP_RETRIES _conn LIST.put
                                ELSE
                        _msg_type RDP_MSG_NACK == IF
                            # --- Handle NACK ---
                            # Peer reports missing packet. NACK seq is the last received seq.
                            # We must resend (NACK_seq + 1).
                            _payload_ptr 1 + AS _tmp_ptr
                            *_tmp_ptr 1 + AS _seq_num

                            # Key is simply the required sequence number
                            _seq_num AS _key

                            RDP_TX_BUF _conn LIST.get AS _tx_buf
                            _key _tx_buf DICT.has_key IF
                                _key _tx_buf DICT.get AS _pkt_buf
                                RDP_PEER_ID    _conn LIST.get AS _dest_id
                                RDP_PEER_PORT  _conn LIST.get AS _dest_port
                                RDP_LOCAL_PORT _conn LIST.get AS _src_port
                                _pkt_buf _dest_id _dest_port _src_port SOCKET.snd_list DROP
                                # Sync approach: Force update from receiver to catch subsequent missing packets
                                _conn RDP_MSG_STAT_REQ _rdp_send_control_packet DROP
                            END
                        ELSE
                        _msg_type RDP_MSG_DATA == IF
                            # --- Handle DATA Packet ---
                            RDP_STATE _conn LIST.get RDP_STATE_OPEN == IF
                                # 1. Extract Sequence Number
                                _payload_ptr 1 + AS _tmp_ptr
                                *_tmp_ptr AS _seq_num

                                # 2. Check Sequence Number against Expected (RDP_SEQ_IN)
                                RDP_SEQ_IN _conn LIST.get AS _expected_seq

                                _seq_num _expected_seq == IF
                                    # Check RX Buffer Capacity (Scenario C)
                                    # If count >= Window Size (simulated via < 1 SWAP -)
                                    RDP_RX_BUF _conn LIST.get DICT.count RDP_RX_WINDOW_SIZE < 1 SWAP - IF
                                        # Buffer Full.
                                        # If not already congested, send WAIT and mark.
                                        RDP_RX_CONGESTED _conn LIST.get 0 == IF
                                            _conn RDP_MSG_WAIT _rdp_send_response_packet DROP
                                            # Mark as congested so we know when to send RESUME later
                                            1 RDP_RX_CONGESTED _conn LIST.put
                                        END
                                    ELSE
                                    # --- In Order Packet ---
                                    # a. Store in Rx_Buffer (Key is seq_num)
                                    _rdp_get_buffer AS _rx_pkt
                                    _rx_pkt 0 != IF
                                        # Copy data from recv_buf to new safe buffer
                                        # Header + Payload
                                        _rx_pkt ARRAY.clear
                                        # Just Copy the whole payload part (which includes our RDP header)
                                        # _payload_ptr points to [Type, Seq, Data...]
                                        # We can iterate and copy.
                                        # Simplified copy for now:
                                        RDP_MSG_DATA _rx_pkt ARRAY.append
                                        _seq_num _rx_pkt ARRAY.append
                                        
                                        # Copy rest of payload
                                        # _payload_ptr points to [Type, Seq, Data...]
                                        # Data starts at _payload_ptr + 2
                                        _rdp_recv_buf MESSAGE.len 2 - AS _len
                                        0 AS _i
                                        WHILE _i _len < DO
                                            _payload_ptr 2 + _i + AS _tmp_ptr
                                            *_tmp_ptr _rx_pkt ARRAY.append
                                            _i 1 + AS _i
                                        DONE
                                        
                                        # Store in Dictionary
                                        _rx_pkt _seq_num 1 + RDP_RX_BUF _conn LIST.get DICT.put
                                    ELSE
                                        &_rdp_err_pool PRTstring HALT
                                    END
                                    
                                    _seq_num 1 + RDP_SEQ_IN _conn LIST.put
                                    
                                    # b. Update Timer (Activity detected)
                                    TIME.uptime RDP_TIMER _conn LIST.put
                                    0 RDP_RETRIES _conn LIST.put

                                ELSE
                                    _seq_num _expected_seq > IF
                                        # --- Out of Order (Missing Packet) ---
                                        # Send NACK for the last correctly received packet (expected - 1)
                                        _conn RDP_MSG_NACK _rdp_send_response_packet DROP
                                    ELSE
                                        # --- Duplicate (seq < expected) ---
                                        # Ignore silently as per spec.
                                    END
                                END
                                    END
                            END
                        END
                        END
                        END
                        END
                        END
                    END
                    END
                    END
                END

            ELSE
                # --- Scenario: No existing connection found ---
                _msg_type RDP_MSG_HELLO == IF
                    # This is a new incoming connection request.
                    # Create a new connection record for the peer.
                    # Use internal alloc to avoid sending a redundant HELLO.
                    _src_id _src_port _local_port _rdp_alloc_conn AS _new_conn
                        
                        # Correctly set the expected incoming sequence number based on the HELLO packet.
                        _payload_ptr 1 + AS _tmp_ptr # Get address of sequence number in payload
                        *_tmp_ptr DUP 
                        RDP_SEQ_IN  _new_conn LIST.put
                        RDP_SEQ_OUT _new_conn LIST.put

                        # We now transition to OPEN and send a STAT_ACK.
                        RDP_STATE_OPEN RDP_STATE _new_conn LIST.put
                        _new_conn RDP_MSG_STAT_ACK _rdp_send_control_packet DROP
                END
            END

        ELSE
            # --- It's an SDP Packet ---
            # TODO: Decide how to handle plain SDP packets.
            # Maybe push them to a separate "unreliable" message queue?
            # For now, we ignore them.
        END
    END

    # 2. Maintenance: Check Timeouts for all active connections
    _rdp_conns DICT.count AS _count
    0 AS _i
    WHILE _i _count < DO
        # DICT.item returns (key value).
        _i _rdp_conns DICT.item AS _conn_ptr AS _key
        
        _conn_ptr _rdp_check_timeout

        RDP_STATE _conn_ptr LIST.get RDP_STATE_CLOSED == IF
            # Connection died, remove it.
            _key _rdp_conns DICT.remove
            _count 1 - AS _count
        ELSE
            _i 1 + AS _i
        END
    DONE
}


# RDP.send ( conn_ptr array_ptr length -- success_flag )
# Sends a block of data reliably over the given connection.
# NOTE: array_ptr must be a pointer to a Heap Array (created with NEW.array).
# This function will handle breaking the data into multiple packets if it
# exceeds the RDP payload size.
DEF RDP.send {
    # Stack: conn_ptr data_ptr length
    AS _len
    AS _data
    AS _conn

    # --- Pre-flight Checks ---
    # 1. Check connection state, data size, and window fullness
    1 AS _can_send
    RDP_STATE _conn LIST.get RDP_STATE_OPEN != IF 0 AS _can_send END
    _len RDP_PACKET_SIZE 2 - > IF 0 AS _can_send END # TODO: Implement packet splitting for large data
    
    RDP_TX_BUF _conn LIST.get AS _tx_buf
    # Check if window is full (count >= window_size). Stacks doesn't have >= or a standalone NOT.
    # We simulate `NOT (count < window_size)` with the expression `1 - (count < window_size)`.
    _tx_buf DICT.count RDP_TX_WINDOW_SIZE < 1 SWAP - IF 0 AS _can_send END

    _can_send IF
        # --- Acquire Resources ---
        _rdp_get_buffer AS _pkt_buf
        _pkt_buf 0 != IF
            # --- Buffer acquired, proceed to build and send ---

            # 1. Get sequence number and destination info from connection record
            RDP_SEQ_OUT _conn LIST.get AS _seq_num
            RDP_PEER_ID _conn LIST.get AS _dest_id
            RDP_PEER_PORT _conn LIST.get AS _dest_port
            RDP_LOCAL_PORT _conn LIST.get AS _src_port

            # 2. Build the packet: Clear buffer, add RDP header
            _pkt_buf ARRAY.clear
            RDP_MSG_DATA _pkt_buf ARRAY.append
            _seq_num _pkt_buf ARRAY.append

            # 3. Copy payload from data_ptr (which is an ARRAY) to the packet buffer
            0 AS _i
            WHILE _i _len < DO
                _i _data ARRAY.get # Get word from source array
                _pkt_buf ARRAY.append
                _i 1 + AS _i
            DONE

            # 4. Send the packet via the socket library
            _pkt_buf _dest_id _dest_port _src_port SOCKET.snd_list
            IF
                # --- Send Success: Update state ---
                # a. Add packet to the Tx_Buffer for potential retransmission
                _pkt_buf _seq_num _tx_buf DICT.put

                # b. Increment the outgoing sequence number for the next packet
                _seq_num 1 + RDP_SEQ_OUT _conn LIST.put

                # c. Update connection timer to reset the timeout
                TIME.uptime RDP_TIMER _conn LIST.put

                # d. If the window is now full, send STAT_REQ and change state
                _tx_buf DICT.count RDP_TX_WINDOW_SIZE == IF
                    _conn RDP_MSG_STAT_REQ _rdp_send_control_packet DROP
                    RDP_STATE_REQ RDP_STATE _conn LIST.put
                END
                1 # Return success
            ELSE
                # --- Send Failure: Cleanup ---
                _pkt_buf _rdp_release_buffer # Return the unused buffer to the pool
                0 # Return failure
            END
        ELSE
            # --- Buffer acquisition failure ---
            0 # Return failure
        END
    ELSE
        # --- Pre-flight check failed ---
        0 # Return failure
    END
}


# RDP.recv ( conn_ptr array_ptr -- success_flag )
# Reads the next available in-order DATA payload from the Rx Buffer into the user's array.
# Returns 1 if data was copied, 0 if no data is available.
# The user array must be large enough to hold the payload.
DEF RDP.recv {
    AS _data
    AS _conn

    VALUE _rx_buf 0
    RDP_RX_BUF _conn LIST.get AS _rx_buf
    
    VALUE _found_pkt 0
    0 AS _found_pkt

    _rx_buf DICT.count AS _count
    
    _count 0 > IF
        # FIFO Strategy: Find the lowest Sequence Number in the buffer
        # 1. Initialize min with the first item's key
        VALUE _min_key 0
        0 _rx_buf DICT.item DROP AS _min_key
        
        # 2. Iterate to find true min
        VALUE _curr_key 0
        1 AS _i
        WHILE _i _count < DO
            _i _rx_buf DICT.item DROP AS _curr_key
            _curr_key _min_key < IF
                _curr_key AS _min_key
            END
            _i 1 + AS _i
        DONE
        
        # 3. Retrieve packet
        _min_key _rx_buf DICT.get AS _pkt_buf
             
             # Copy data to user array (Offset 2 is start of data in our packet format [Type, Seq, Data...])
             # _pkt_buf contains [Capacity, Count, Type, Seq, Payload...]
             # User array _data contains [Capacity, Count, Payload...]
             # Payload starts at offset 2 in _pkt_buf (Type, Seq)
             # Payload starts at offset 0 in user array (APPEND)
             _pkt_buf ARRAY.len 2 - AS _len
             0 AS _j
             WHILE _j _len < DO
                 _j 2 + _pkt_buf ARRAY.get _data ARRAY.append
                 _j 1 + AS _j
             DONE
             
             # Cleanup
             _pkt_buf _rdp_release_buffer
             _min_key _rx_buf DICT.remove
             
             # Flow Control Hysteresis (Low Watermark)
             # Only send RESUME if we were congested AND we now have room for a full TX Window.
             # Threshold: Count <= (RX_SIZE - TX_SIZE) -> 10 - 6 = 4.
             RDP_RX_CONGESTED _conn LIST.get 1 == IF
                 _rx_buf DICT.count 5 < IF
                     0 RDP_RX_CONGESTED _conn LIST.put
                     _conn RDP_MSG_RESUME _rdp_send_response_packet DROP
                 END
             END
             
             1 AS _found_pkt
    END
    
    _found_pkt
}

# RDP.print_status ( -- )
# Prints the internal status of all active connections for debugging.
DEF RDP.print_status {
    &_str_rdp_status PRTstring
    _rdp_conns DICT.count AS _count
    &_str_active_conn PRTstring _count PRTnum &_str_newline PRTstring
    
    0 AS _i
    WHILE _i _count < DO
        _i _rdp_conns DICT.item AS _conn_ptr DROP # Get value (conn_ptr), drop key
        
        &_str_conn PRTstring _i PRTnum &_str_colon PRTstring
        &_str_state PRTstring RDP_STATE _conn_ptr LIST.get PRTnum
        &_str_seq_out PRTstring RDP_SEQ_OUT _conn_ptr LIST.get PRTnum
        &_str_seq_in PRTstring RDP_SEQ_IN _conn_ptr LIST.get PRTnum
        &_str_newline PRTstring
        
        &_str_tx_buf PRTstring 
        RDP_TX_BUF _conn_ptr LIST.get DICT.count PRTnum
        
        &_str_rx_buf PRTstring 
        RDP_RX_BUF _conn_ptr LIST.get DICT.count PRTnum
        &_str_newline PRTstring
        
        &_str_timer PRTstring 
        RDP_TIMER _conn_ptr LIST.get PRTnum
        &_str_retries PRTstring 
        RDP_RETRIES _conn_ptr LIST.get PRTnum
        &_str_newline PRTstring

        _i 1 + AS _i
    DONE
    &_str_rdp_footer PRTstring
}

FILE: src/libs/socket_lib.stacks
------------------------------------------------------------
# socket_lib - User-space API for Sternnet
# This library provides a high-level, safe interface for applications
# to interact with the kernel's network stack.

USE std_string
USE std_deque
USE std_heap

# --- Static TX Buffer ---
# We use a single static buffer for sending to avoid heap fragmentation.
# LIST _send_buffer 256
VALUE _send_buffer 0

# --- Syscall IDs ---
# CONST SYS_NET_CONFIG 65   #We do not need thhes CONST, are already ASM symbols
# CONST SYS_NET_BIND 60
# CONST SYS_NET_CONFIG 65
# CONST INT_VECTORS 10
# CONST SYS_NET_BIND 60
# CONST SYS_NET_SEND 61
# CONST SYS_NET_CONFIG 65
# CONST INT_VECTORS 10


# --- Library Functions ---

# ( host_id rx_buffer_size -- success )
DEF SOCKET.init {
    ASM {
        ldi I ~SYS_NET_CONFIG ; syscall 65
        int $INT_VECTORS
    }
    256 NEW.list AS _send_buffer
}

# ( array_ptr deque_ptr -- success_flag )
# NOTE: The array_ptr is expected to be a dynamic array from std_heap.
# The function will overwrite the array's content and update its count.
DEF SOCKET.read {
    VALUE _read_deque 0
    AS _read_deque
    VALUE _user_buf 0
    AS _user_buf

    # 1. Get user buffer capacity from its header
    VALUE _user_buf_len 0
    *_user_buf AS _user_buf_len # Read capacity from array[0]

    # 1. Trigger Kernel Poll (Syscall 62)
    # This moves packets from HAL to Deques if available
    ASM {
        ldi I ~SYS_NET_RECV
        int $INT_VECTORS
    }

    # 2. Check application mailbox
    _read_deque DEQUE.is_empty IF
        0 # Return Failure (No Data)
    ELSE
        # 3. Retrieve Kernel Buffer
        VALUE _kern_pkt 0
        _read_deque DEQUE.pop AS _kern_pkt

        # 4. Calculate Copy Size
        # Envelope: [SrcID(1), DestPort(1), SrcPort(1), PayLen(1), Payload...]
        # We want to copy the whole envelope (Header 4 + Payload)
        VALUE _payload_len 0
        VALUE _tmp_ptr 0
        _kern_pkt 3 + AS _tmp_ptr # Offset 3 has length
        *_tmp_ptr AS _payload_len
        
        VALUE _total_len 0
        _payload_len 4 + AS _total_len

        VALUE _copy_len 0
        _total_len AS _copy_len
        _copy_len _user_buf_len > IF
            _user_buf_len AS _copy_len
        END

        # 5. Copy Loop (Kernel -> User's Array Data Section)
        # The data section of a dynamic array starts at offset 2.
        VALUE _user_buf_data_ptr 0
        _user_buf 2 + AS _user_buf_data_ptr

        VALUE _ri 0
        0 AS _ri
        VALUE _src 0
        VALUE _dst 0

        WHILE _ri _copy_len < DO
            _kern_pkt _ri + AS _src
            _user_buf_data_ptr _ri + AS _dst
            *_src AS *_dst
            _ri 1 + AS _ri
        DONE

        # 6. Release Kernel Resource (Syscall 64)
        _kern_pkt ASM { 
            ldi I ~SYS_NET_FREE 
            int $INT_VECTORS 
        }

        # 7. Update the user array's count field
        VALUE _user_buf_count_ptr 0
        _user_buf 1 + AS _user_buf_count_ptr
        _copy_len AS *_user_buf_count_ptr

        1 # Return Success
    END
}

# ( str_ptr dest_id dest_port src_port -- success )
DEF SOCKET.snd_text {
    VALUE _src_port 0
    AS _src_port

    VALUE _dest_port 0
    AS _dest_port

    VALUE _dest_id 0
    AS _dest_id

    VALUE _str_ptr 0
    AS _str_ptr
    
    VALUE _char_ptr 0

    # 1. Calculate Payload Length
    _str_ptr STRlen AS _payload_len

    # 2. Safety Check (Max Payload = 240 words)
    _payload_len 240 > IF
        0 # Return Failure (Too large)
    ELSE
        # 3. Populate the static _send_buffer
        # Layout: [DestID, DestPort, SrcPort, Length, Payload...]
        _send_buffer AS _tmp_ptr
        
        _dest_id     AS *_tmp_ptr
        _tmp_ptr 1 + AS _tmp_ptr
        _dest_port   AS *_tmp_ptr
        _tmp_ptr 1 + AS _tmp_ptr
        _src_port    AS *_tmp_ptr
        _tmp_ptr 1 + AS _tmp_ptr
        _payload_len AS *_tmp_ptr
        _tmp_ptr 1 + AS _tmp_ptr

        # 4. Copy Payload
        # VALUE _i 0;       # We reuse _i here, is a (smal risk)
        0 AS _i
        WHILE _i _payload_len < DO
            # Calculate source address and get char
            _str_ptr _i + AS _char_ptr
            *_char_ptr
            # Store in buffer (Offset 4)
            AS *_tmp_ptr
            _tmp_ptr 1 + AS _tmp_ptr
            _i 1 + AS _i
        DONE

        # 5. Call Syscall with pointer to buffer
        _send_buffer
        ASM {
            ldi I ~SYS_NET_SEND
            int $INT_VECTORS
        }
    END
}



# ( num dest_id dest_port src_port -- success )
DEF SOCKET.snd_num {
    # VALUE _src_port 0     ; already defined in snd_text
    AS _src_port
    # VALUE _dest_port 0    ; already defined
    AS _dest_port
    # VALUE _dest_id 0      ; already defined
    AS _dest_id
    VALUE _num 0
    AS _num

    0 AS _payload_len
    # VALUE _payload_len 0  ; already defined
    VALUE _p_ptr 0
    _send_buffer 4 + AS _p_ptr

    # 1. Handle Negative Numbers
    _num 0 < IF
        45 AS *_p_ptr      # Write '-'
        _p_ptr 1 + AS _p_ptr
        _payload_len 1 + AS _payload_len
        _num NEGATE AS _num   # Make positive for digit extraction
    END

    # 2. Convert to ASCII
    _num 0 == IF
        48 AS *_p_ptr      # Just write '0'
        _payload_len 1 + AS _payload_len
    ELSE
        # Extract digits to stack (reverse order)
        VALUE _digit_count 0
        0 AS _digit_count
        WHILE _num 0 > DO
            _num 10 % 48 + # Get ASCII digit
            _num 10 // AS _num
            _digit_count 1 + AS _digit_count
        DONE
        # Pop from stack to buffer (correct order)
        WHILE _digit_count 0 > DO
            AS *_p_ptr
            _p_ptr 1 + AS _p_ptr
            _payload_len 1 + AS _payload_len
            _digit_count 1 - AS _digit_count
        DONE
    END

    # 3. Populate headers in _send_buffer
    # Layout: [DestID, DestPort, SrcPort, Length, Payload...]
    _send_buffer AS _tmp_ptr
    _dest_id     AS *_tmp_ptr
    _tmp_ptr 1 + AS _tmp_ptr
    _dest_port   AS *_tmp_ptr
    _tmp_ptr 1 + AS _tmp_ptr
    _src_port    AS *_tmp_ptr
    _tmp_ptr 1 + AS _tmp_ptr
    _payload_len AS *_tmp_ptr

    # 4. Call Syscall
    _send_buffer
    ASM {
        ldi I ~SYS_NET_SEND
        int $INT_VECTORS
    }
}


# ( list_ptr dest_id dest_port src_port -- success )
# Sends a payload from a heap-allocated array (created with NEW.array).
DEF SOCKET.snd_list {
    # Reusing globals defined in SOCKET.snd_text and SOCKET.read
    AS _src_port
    AS _dest_port
    AS _dest_id
    
    VALUE _snd_list_ptr 0
    AS _snd_list_ptr

    # 1. Get payload length from array header
    _snd_list_ptr ARRAY.len AS _payload_len

    # 2. Safety Check (Max Payload = 240 words)
    _payload_len 240 > IF
        0 # Return Failure
    ELSE
        # 3. Populate headers in _send_buffer
        _send_buffer AS _tmp_ptr
        _dest_id     AS *_tmp_ptr
        _tmp_ptr 1 + AS _tmp_ptr
        _dest_port   AS *_tmp_ptr
        _tmp_ptr 1 + AS _tmp_ptr
        _src_port    AS *_tmp_ptr
        _tmp_ptr 1 + AS _tmp_ptr
        _payload_len AS *_tmp_ptr
        _tmp_ptr 1 + AS _tmp_ptr # _tmp_ptr now points to payload start

        # 4. Copy Payload from list
        0 AS _i
        WHILE _i _payload_len < DO
            _i _snd_list_ptr ARRAY.get  # Get value from array
            AS *_tmp_ptr            # Store in buffer
            _tmp_ptr 1 + AS _tmp_ptr
            _i 1 + AS _i
        DONE

        # 5. Call Syscall
        _send_buffer
        ASM {
            ldi I ~SYS_NET_SEND
            int $INT_VECTORS
            nop
        }
    END
}





# ( port_id deque_ptr -- )
DEF SOCKET.bind {
    ASM {
        ldi I ~SYS_NET_BIND ; syscall 60
        int $INT_VECTORS
    }
}



# --- MESSAGE Helper Methods ---
# These methods operate on the array returned/filled by SOCKET.read.
# Note: They account for the heap-array header (Capacity at index 0, Count at index 1).
# The Envelope data starts at index 2 of the raw pointer.

VALUE _length 0
VALUE _ptr 0


# ( message_ptr -- source_id )
DEF MESSAGE.src {
    2 + AS _tmp_ptr
    *_tmp_ptr
}

# ( message_ptr -- dest_port )
DEF MESSAGE.dest_port {
    2 + 1 + AS _tmp_ptr
    *_tmp_ptr
}

# ( message_ptr -- src_port )
DEF MESSAGE.src_port {
    2 + 2 + AS _tmp_ptr
    *_tmp_ptr
}

# ( message_ptr -- payload_len )
DEF MESSAGE.len {
    2 + 3 + AS _tmp_ptr
    *_tmp_ptr
}

# ( message_ptr -- payload_ptr )
DEF MESSAGE.payload_ptr {
    2 + 4 +
}

# ( message_ptr -- payload_ptr )
# Adds a null terminator after the payload and returns the pointer to the string.
DEF MESSAGE.as_string {
    VALUE _msg 0
    AS _msg
    
    _msg MESSAGE.len AS _length
    _msg MESSAGE.payload_ptr AS _ptr
    
    # Add null terminator at ptr + length
    # Note: This modifies the buffer in-place.
    VALUE _term_ptr 0
    _ptr _length + AS _term_ptr
    0 AS *_term_ptr
    
    _ptr # Return the string pointer
}


# ( message_ptr -- num )
# Converts the ASCII payload of a message back into a signed integer.
DEF MESSAGE.as_num {
    # VALUE _msg 0          ; defined in MESSAGE.as_string
    AS _msg
    _msg MESSAGE.len AS _length
    _msg MESSAGE.payload_ptr AS _ptr

    VALUE _res 0
    0 AS _res
    VALUE _is_neg 0
    0 AS _is_neg
    # 0 AS _i               ; defined in SOCKET.snd_text
    0 AS _i
    VALUE _curr_ptr 0
    VALUE _val 0

    # 1. Handle Sign
    _length 0 > IF
        *_ptr 45 == IF      # ASCII '-'
            1 AS _is_neg
            1 AS _i
        END
    END

    # 2. Convert digits
    WHILE _i _length < DO
        _ptr _i + AS _curr_ptr
        *_curr_ptr 
        AS _val
        
        _val 47 > IF 
            _val 58 < IF
                _res 10 * 
                _val 48 - + AS _res
            END
        END
        _i 1 + AS _i
    DONE

    # 3. Apply sign and return
    _is_neg IF 0 _res - ELSE _res END
}

FILE: src/libs/std_deque.stacks
------------------------------------------------------------
# std_deque.stacks 
# Double-Ended Queue (Deque) with Dynamic Node Pool (Slab Allocator)
# Requires: std_heap

USE std_heap

# --- Configuration ---
CONST DEQUE_NODE_SIZE 3
CONST DEQUE_OFF_VAL 0
CONST DEQUE_OFF_NEXT 1
CONST DEQUE_OFF_PREV 2

CONST DEQUE_CTRL_HEAD 0
CONST DEQUE_CTRL_TAIL 1

VALUE DEQUE_FREE_HEAD 0
VALUE DEQUE_POOL_PAGE_SIZE 0

# Internal Variables
VALUE _dq_i 0
VALUE _dq_ptr 0
VALUE _dq_next_ptr 0
VALUE _dq_node 0
VALUE _dq_val 0
VALUE _dq_list 0
VALUE _dq_head 0
VALUE _dq_tail 0
VALUE _dq_prev 0
VALUE _dq_next 0

STRING _dq_err_empty "DEQUE.pop: Deque is empty\n"

# --- Pool Management ---

DEF _DEQUE.grow_pool {
    # Allocate block
    DEQUE_POOL_PAGE_SIZE DEQUE_NODE_SIZE * NEW.list AS _dq_ptr
    
    # Link nodes
    0 AS _dq_i
    WHILE _dq_i DEQUE_POOL_PAGE_SIZE 1 - < DO
        # Current node address: _dq_ptr + (_dq_i * 3)
        # Next node address:    _dq_ptr + ((_dq_i + 1) * 3)
        
        _dq_ptr _dq_i DEQUE_NODE_SIZE * + AS _dq_node
        _dq_ptr _dq_i 1 + DEQUE_NODE_SIZE * + AS _dq_next_ptr
        
        _dq_next_ptr DEQUE_OFF_NEXT _dq_node LIST.put
        
        _dq_i 1 + AS _dq_i
    DONE
    
    # Link last node to current free head
    _dq_ptr _dq_i DEQUE_NODE_SIZE * + AS _dq_node
    DEQUE_FREE_HEAD DEQUE_OFF_NEXT _dq_node LIST.put
    
    # Update free head to start of new block
    _dq_ptr AS DEQUE_FREE_HEAD
}

DEF DEQUE.init_pool {
    AS DEQUE_POOL_PAGE_SIZE
    0 AS DEQUE_FREE_HEAD
    _DEQUE.grow_pool
}

DEF _DEQUE.alloc_node {
    DEQUE_FREE_HEAD 0 == IF
        _DEQUE.grow_pool
    END
    
    DEQUE_FREE_HEAD AS _dq_node
    
    # Update free head -> node.next
    DEQUE_OFF_NEXT _dq_node LIST.get AS DEQUE_FREE_HEAD
    
    # Clear pointers for safety
    0 DEQUE_OFF_NEXT _dq_node LIST.put
    0 DEQUE_OFF_PREV _dq_node LIST.put
    
    _dq_node
}

DEF _DEQUE.free_node {
    AS _dq_node
    # node.next = free_head
    DEQUE_FREE_HEAD DEQUE_OFF_NEXT _dq_node LIST.put
    # free_head = node
    _dq_node AS DEQUE_FREE_HEAD
}

# --- Deque Controller ---

DEF DEQUE.new {
    # Allocate controller [Head, Tail]
    2 NEW.list AS _dq_list
    0 DEQUE_CTRL_HEAD _dq_list LIST.put
    0 DEQUE_CTRL_TAIL _dq_list LIST.put
    _dq_list
}

DEF DEQUE.is_empty {
    AS _dq_list
    DEQUE_CTRL_HEAD _dq_list LIST.get 0 ==
}

# --- Insertion ---

DEF DEQUE.push {
    AS _dq_list
    AS _dq_val
    
    _DEQUE.alloc_node AS _dq_node
    _dq_val DEQUE_OFF_VAL _dq_node LIST.put
    
    DEQUE_CTRL_HEAD _dq_list LIST.get AS _dq_head
    
    # node.next = head
    _dq_head DEQUE_OFF_NEXT _dq_node LIST.put
    # node.prev = 0
    0 DEQUE_OFF_PREV _dq_node LIST.put
    
    _dq_head 0 != IF
        # head.prev = node
        _dq_node DEQUE_OFF_PREV _dq_head LIST.put
    ELSE
        # List was empty, tail = node
        _dq_node DEQUE_CTRL_TAIL _dq_list LIST.put
    END
    
    # head = node
    _dq_node DEQUE_CTRL_HEAD _dq_list LIST.put
}

DEF DEQUE.append {
    AS _dq_list
    AS _dq_val
    
    _DEQUE.alloc_node AS _dq_node
    _dq_val DEQUE_OFF_VAL _dq_node LIST.put
    
    DEQUE_CTRL_TAIL _dq_list LIST.get AS _dq_tail
    
    # node.prev = tail
    _dq_tail DEQUE_OFF_PREV _dq_node LIST.put
    # node.next = 0
    0 DEQUE_OFF_NEXT _dq_node LIST.put
    
    _dq_tail 0 != IF
        # tail.next = node
        _dq_node DEQUE_OFF_NEXT _dq_tail LIST.put
    ELSE
        # List was empty, head = node
        _dq_node DEQUE_CTRL_HEAD _dq_list LIST.put
    END
    
    # tail = node
    _dq_node DEQUE_CTRL_TAIL _dq_list LIST.put
}

# --- Removal ---

DEF DEQUE.pop {
    AS _dq_list
    
    DEQUE_CTRL_HEAD _dq_list LIST.get AS _dq_head
    
    _dq_head 0 == IF
        &_dq_err_empty PRTstring HALT
    END
    
    DEQUE_OFF_VAL _dq_head LIST.get AS _dq_val
    DEQUE_OFF_NEXT _dq_head LIST.get AS _dq_next
    
    # head = next
    _dq_next DEQUE_CTRL_HEAD _dq_list LIST.put
    
    _dq_next 0 != IF
        # next.prev = 0
        0 DEQUE_OFF_PREV _dq_next LIST.put
    ELSE
        # List empty, tail = 0
        0 DEQUE_CTRL_TAIL _dq_list LIST.put
    END
    
    _dq_head _DEQUE.free_node
    _dq_val
}

DEF DEQUE.pop_tail {
    AS _dq_list
    
    DEQUE_CTRL_TAIL _dq_list LIST.get AS _dq_tail
    
    _dq_tail 0 == IF
        &_dq_err_empty PRTstring HALT
    END
    
    DEQUE_OFF_VAL  _dq_tail LIST.get AS _dq_val
    DEQUE_OFF_PREV _dq_tail LIST.get AS _dq_prev
    
    # tail = prev
    _dq_prev DEQUE_CTRL_TAIL _dq_list LIST.put
    
    _dq_prev 0 != IF
        # prev.next = 0
        0 DEQUE_OFF_NEXT _dq_prev LIST.put
    ELSE
        # List empty, head = 0
        0 DEQUE_CTRL_HEAD _dq_list LIST.put
    END
    
    _dq_tail _DEQUE.free_node
    _dq_val
}

# --- Traversal ---

DEF DEQUE.head {
    DEQUE_CTRL_HEAD SWAP LIST.get
}

DEF DEQUE.tail {
    DEQUE_CTRL_TAIL SWAP LIST.get
}

DEF DEQUE.is_last {
    # ( node_ptr -- bool )
    DEQUE_OFF_NEXT SWAP LIST.get 0 ==
}

DEF DEQUE.is_first {
    # ( node_ptr -- bool )
    DEQUE_OFF_PREV SWAP LIST.get 0 ==
}

DEF DEQUE.next {
    DEQUE_OFF_NEXT SWAP LIST.get
}

DEF DEQUE.prev {
    DEQUE_OFF_PREV SWAP LIST.get
}

DEF DEQUE.value {
    DEQUE_OFF_VAL SWAP LIST.get
}

FILE: src/libs/std_dict.stacks
------------------------------------------------------------
# std_dict.stacks
# Linear Dictionary Library
# Requires: std_heap

USE std_heap

# --- Configuration ---
CONST _DICT_OFF_CAP 0
CONST _DICT_OFF_CNT 1
CONST _DICT_HDR_SZ 2

# Internal Variables
VALUE _dict_ptr 0
VALUE _dict_cap 0
VALUE _dict_cnt 0
VALUE _dict_key 0
VALUE _dict_val 0
VALUE _dict_idx 0
VALUE _dict_found 0
VALUE _dict_offset 0
VALUE _dict_last_off 0
VALUE _dict_last_key 0
VALUE _dict_last_val 0

STRING _dict_err_full "DICT.put: Dictionary is full\n"
STRING _dict_err_key  "DICT.get: Key not found\n"
STRING _dict_err_bnd  "DICT.item: Index out of bounds\n"
STRING _dict_err_inv_key "DICT.put: Key 0 is reserved and cannot be used.\n"

# --- DICT.new ---
# Creates a new dictionary
# Stack: ( capacity -- dict_ptr )
DEF DICT.new {
    AS _dict_cap
    
    # Allocate: Header (2) + Capacity * 2
    _dict_cap 2 * _DICT_HDR_SZ + NEW.list AS _dict_ptr
    
    # Store Capacity
    _dict_cap _DICT_OFF_CAP _dict_ptr LIST.put
    
    # Store Count (0)
    0 _DICT_OFF_CNT _dict_ptr LIST.put
    
    _dict_ptr
}

# --- DICT.count ---
# Returns number of items
# Stack: ( dict_ptr -- count )
DEF DICT.count {
    _DICT_OFF_CNT SWAP LIST.get
}

# --- DICT.put ---
# Adds or updates a key-value pair
# Stack: ( value key dict_ptr -- )
DEF DICT.put {
    AS _dict_ptr
    AS _dict_key
    AS _dict_val
    
    _dict_key 0 == IF
        &_dict_err_inv_key PRTstring HALT
    END
    
    _DICT_OFF_CNT _dict_ptr LIST.get AS _dict_cnt
    
    0 AS _dict_found
    0 AS _dict_idx
    
    # Linear scan to check if key exists
    WHILE _dict_idx _dict_cnt < DO
        # Offset = 2 + idx * 2
        _dict_idx 2 * _DICT_HDR_SZ + AS _dict_offset
        
        # Check Key
        _dict_offset _dict_ptr LIST.get _dict_key == IF
            # Found match. Update Value (Offset + 1)
            _dict_val _dict_offset 1 + _dict_ptr LIST.put
            1 AS _dict_found
            # Exit loop
            _dict_cnt AS _dict_idx
        ELSE
            _dict_idx 1 + AS _dict_idx
        END
    DONE
    
    _dict_found 0 == IF
        # Not found, add new
        _DICT_OFF_CAP _dict_ptr LIST.get AS _dict_cap
        
        _dict_cnt _dict_cap == IF
            &_dict_err_full PRTstring HALT
        END
        
        # Add at end: Offset = 2 + count * 2
        _dict_cnt 2 * _DICT_HDR_SZ + AS _dict_offset
        _dict_key _dict_offset _dict_ptr LIST.put
        _dict_val _dict_offset 1 + _dict_ptr LIST.put
        
        # Increment Count
        _dict_cnt 1 + _DICT_OFF_CNT _dict_ptr LIST.put
    END
}

# --- DICT.get ---
# Retrieves a value by key
# Stack: ( key dict_ptr -- value )
DEF DICT.get {
    AS _dict_ptr
    AS _dict_key
    
    _DICT_OFF_CNT _dict_ptr LIST.get AS _dict_cnt
    
    0 AS _dict_found
    0 AS _dict_idx
    
    WHILE _dict_idx _dict_cnt < DO
        _dict_idx 2 * _DICT_HDR_SZ + AS _dict_offset
        
        _dict_offset _dict_ptr LIST.get _dict_key == IF
            # Found match. Get Value
            _dict_offset 1 + _dict_ptr LIST.get
            1 AS _dict_found
            # Exit loop
            _dict_cnt AS _dict_idx
        ELSE
            _dict_idx 1 + AS _dict_idx
        END
    DONE
    
    _dict_found 0 == IF
        &_dict_err_key PRTstring HALT
    END
}

# --- DICT.has_key ---
# Checks if key exists
# Stack: ( key dict_ptr -- bool )
DEF DICT.has_key {
    AS _dict_ptr
    AS _dict_key
    
    _DICT_OFF_CNT _dict_ptr LIST.get AS _dict_cnt
    
    0 AS _dict_found
    0 AS _dict_idx
    
    WHILE _dict_idx _dict_cnt < DO
        _dict_idx 2 * _DICT_HDR_SZ + AS _dict_offset
        
        _dict_offset _dict_ptr LIST.get _dict_key == IF
            1 AS _dict_found
            _dict_cnt AS _dict_idx
        ELSE
            _dict_idx 1 + AS _dict_idx
